<t>CREATE TABLE scores ( score_id INT PRIMARY KEY, player_id INT, game_id INT, score INT, FOREIGN KEY (player_id) REFERENCES players(player_id), FOREIGN KEY (game_id) REFERENCES games(game_id) );

<t>CREATE TABLE Game ( game_id INT PRIMARY KEY, title VARCHAR(255), genre VARCHAR(50), release_date DATE, platform VARCHAR(50) );

CREATE TABLE Player ( player_id INT PRIMARY KEY, player_name VARCHAR(255), email VARCHAR(255), date_of_birth DATE, country VARCHAR(50) );

CREATE TABLE Scoreboard ( game_id INT, player_id INT, score INT, level INT, PRIMARY KEY (game_id, player_id), FOREIGN KEY (game_id) REFERENCES Game(game_id), FOREIGN KEY (player_id) REFERENCES Player(player_id) );

CREATE TABLE GameReview ( review_id INT PRIMARY KEY, game_id INT, player_id INT, rating FLOAT, review_text TEXT, FOREIGN KEY (game_id) REFERENCES Game(game_id), FOREIGN KEY (player_id) REFERENCES Player(player_id) );</t><s>INSERT INTO Game (game_id, title, genre, release_date, platform) VALUES (1, 'Super Mario Odyssey', 'Action-Adventure', '2017-10-27', 'Nintendo Switch') ON DUPLICATE KEY UPDATE title='Super Mario Odyssey', genre='Action-Adventure', release_date='2017-10-27', platform='Nintendo Switch';</s>

CREATE TABLE Game ( game_id INT PRIMARY KEY, title VARCHAR(255), genre VARCHAR(50), release_date DATE, platform VARCHAR(50) );</t><s>insert into game (game_id, title, genre, release_date, platform) values (1, 'super mario odyssey', 'action-adventure', '2017-10-27', 'nintendo switch') on duplicate key update title='super mario odyssey', genre='action-adventure', release_date='2017-10-27', platform='nintendo switch';</s>

CREATE TABLE GameReview ( review_id INT PRIMARY KEY, game_id INT, player_id INT, rating FLOAT, review_text TEXT, FOREIGN KEY (game_id) REFERENCES Game(game_id), FOREIGN KEY (player_id) REFERENCES Player(player_id) );</t><s>INSERT INTO Player (player_id, player_name, email, date_of_birth, country) VALUES (1, 'John Doe', 'john.doe@example.com', '1990-05-15', 'US') ON DUPLICATE KEY UPDATE player_name='John Doe', email='john.doe@example.com', date_of_birth='1990-05-15', country='US';</s>

CREATE TABLE Scoreboard ( game_id INT, player_id INT, score INT, level INT, PRIMARY KEY (game_id, player_id), FOREIGN KEY (game_id) REFERENCES Game(game_id), FOREIGN KEY (player_id) REFERENCES Player(player_id) );</t><s>INSERT INTO Scoreboard (game_id, player_id, score, level) VALUES (1, 1, 1000, 10) ON DUPLICATE KEY UPDATE score=1000, level=10;</s>

CREATE TABLE Game (GameID INT PRIMARY KEY, GameName VARCHAR(50), ReleaseDate DATE, Genre VARCHAR(50), Platform VARCHAR(50);

CREATE TABLE GameReview (ReviewID INT PRIMARY KEY, GameID INT, PlayerID INT, Rating INT, ReviewText TEXT, FOREIGN KEY (GameID) REFERENCES Game(GameID), FOREIGN KEY (PlayerID) REFERENCES Player(PlayerID));

CREATE TABLE PlayerInventory (InventoryID INT PRIMARY KEY, PlayerID INT, ItemName VARCHAR(50), Quantity INT, FOREIGN KEY (PlayerID) REFERENCES Player(PlayerID));

CREATE TABLE PlayerGameHistory (PlayerID INT, GameID INT, PlayTimeInHours INT, Score INT, FOREIGN KEY (PlayerID) REFERENCES Player(PlayerID), FOREIGN KEY (GameID) REFERENCES Game(GameID));</t><s>upsert into player (playerid, playername, age, email, highscore) values (1, 'john doe', 25, 'john.doe@example.com', 1000) on duplicate key update playername = 'john doe', age = 25, email = 'john.doe@example.com', highscore = 1000;</s>

CREATE TABLE PlayerInventory (InventoryID INT PRIMARY KEY, PlayerID INT, ItemName VARCHAR(50), Quantity INT, FOREIGN KEY (PlayerID) REFERENCES Player(PlayerID));</t><s>UPSERT INTO Player (PlayerID, PlayerName, Age, Email, HighScore) VALUES (1, 'John Doe', 25, 'john.doe@example.com', 1000) ON DUPLICATE KEY UPDATE PlayerName = 'John Doe', Age = 25, Email = 'john.doe@example.com', HighScore = 1000;</s>

CREATE TABLE GameReview (ReviewID INT PRIMARY KEY, GameID INT, PlayerID INT, Rating INT, ReviewText TEXT, FOREIGN KEY (GameID) REFERENCES Game(GameID), FOREIGN KEY (PlayerID) REFERENCES Player(PlayerID));</t><s>upsert into player (playerid, playername, age, email, highscore) values (1, 'john doe', 25, 'john.doe@example.com', 1000) on duplicate key update playername = 'john doe', age = 25, email = 'john.doe@example.com', highscore = 1000;</s>
<t>CREATE TABLE Game (GameID INT PRIMARY KEY, GameName VARCHAR(50), ReleaseDate DATE, Genre VARCHAR(50), Platform VARCHAR(50);

CREATE TABLE PlayerGameHistory (PlayerID INT, GameID INT, PlayTimeInHours INT, Score INT, FOREIGN KEY (PlayerID) REFERENCES Player(PlayerID), FOREIGN KEY (GameID) REFERENCES Game(GameID));</t><s>UPSERT INTO Player (PlayerID, PlayerName, Age, Email, HighScore) VALUES (1, 'John Doe', 25, 'john.doe@example.com', 1000) ON DUPLICATE KEY UPDATE PlayerName = 'John Doe', Age = 25, Email = 'john.doe@example.com', HighScore = 1000;</s>
<t>CREATE TABLE Game (GameID INT PRIMARY KEY, GameName VARCHAR(50), ReleaseDate DATE, Genre VARCHAR(50), Platform VARCHAR(50);

CREATE TABLE PlayerInventory (InventoryID INT PRIMARY KEY, PlayerID INT, ItemName VARCHAR(50), Quantity INT, FOREIGN KEY (PlayerID) REFERENCES Player(PlayerID));</t><s>upsert into player (playerid, playername, age, email, highscore) values (1, 'john doe', 25, 'john.doe@example.com', 1000) on duplicate key update playername = 'john doe', age = 25, email = 'john.doe@example.com', highscore = 1000;</s>
<t>CREATE TABLE PlayerGameHistory (PlayerID INT, GameID INT, PlayTimeInHours INT, Score INT, FOREIGN KEY (PlayerID) REFERENCES Player(PlayerID), FOREIGN KEY (GameID) REFERENCES Game(GameID));

CREATE TABLE PlayerInventory (InventoryID INT PRIMARY KEY, PlayerID INT, ItemName VARCHAR(50), Quantity INT, FOREIGN KEY (PlayerID) REFERENCES Player(PlayerID));

CREATE TABLE Player (PlayerID INT PRIMARY KEY, PlayerName VARCHAR(50), Age INT, Email VARCHAR(50), HighScore INT);</t><s>UPSERT INTO Player (PlayerID, PlayerName, Age, Email, HighScore) VALUES (1, 'John Doe', 25, 'john.doe@example.com', 1000) ON DUPLICATE KEY UPDATE PlayerName = 'John Doe', Age = 25, Email = 'john.doe@example.com', HighScore = 1000;</s>
<t>CREATE TABLE PlayerInventory (InventoryID INT PRIMARY KEY, PlayerID INT, ItemName VARCHAR(50), Quantity INT, FOREIGN KEY (PlayerID) REFERENCES Player(PlayerID));

CREATE TABLE GameReview (ReviewID INT PRIMARY KEY, GameID INT, PlayerID INT, Rating INT, ReviewText TEXT, FOREIGN KEY (GameID) REFERENCES Game(GameID), FOREIGN KEY (PlayerID) REFERENCES Player(PlayerID));</t><s>upsert into game (gameid, gamename, releasedate, genre, platform) values (1, 'example game 1', '2022-01-01', 'action', 'pc') on duplicate key update gamename = 'example game 1', releasedate = '2022-01-01', genre = 'action', platform = 'pc';</s>

CREATE TABLE PlayerGameHistory (PlayerID INT, GameID INT, PlayTimeInHours INT, Score INT, FOREIGN KEY (PlayerID) REFERENCES Player(PlayerID), FOREIGN KEY (GameID) REFERENCES Game(GameID));</t><s>UPSERT INTO Game (GameID, GameName, ReleaseDate, Genre, Platform) VALUES (1, 'Example Game 1', '2022-01-01', 'Action', 'PC') ON DUPLICATE KEY UPDATE GameName = 'Example Game 1', ReleaseDate = '2022-01-01', Genre = 'Action', Platform = 'PC';</s>

CREATE TABLE Game (GameID INT PRIMARY KEY, GameName VARCHAR(50), ReleaseDate DATE, Genre VARCHAR(50), Platform VARCHAR(50);

CREATE TABLE PlayerInventory (InventoryID INT PRIMARY KEY, PlayerID INT, ItemName VARCHAR(50), Quantity INT, FOREIGN KEY (PlayerID) REFERENCES Player(PlayerID));</t><s>UPSERT INTO Game (GameID, GameName, ReleaseDate, Genre, Platform) VALUES (1, 'Example Game 1', '2022-01-01', 'Action', 'PC') ON DUPLICATE KEY UPDATE GameName = 'Example Game 1', ReleaseDate = '2022-01-01', Genre = 'Action', Platform = 'PC';</s>

CREATE TABLE PlayerGameHistory (PlayerID INT, GameID INT, PlayTimeInHours INT, Score INT, FOREIGN KEY (PlayerID) REFERENCES Player(PlayerID), FOREIGN KEY (GameID) REFERENCES Game(GameID));

CREATE TABLE Player (PlayerID INT PRIMARY KEY, PlayerName VARCHAR(50), Age INT, Email VARCHAR(50), HighScore INT);

CREATE TABLE PlayerInventory (InventoryID INT PRIMARY KEY, PlayerID INT, ItemName VARCHAR(50), Quantity INT, FOREIGN KEY (PlayerID) REFERENCES Player(PlayerID));

CREATE TABLE Game (GameID INT PRIMARY KEY, GameName VARCHAR(50), ReleaseDate DATE, Genre VARCHAR(50), Platform VARCHAR(50);

CREATE TABLE Player (PlayerID INT PRIMARY KEY, PlayerName VARCHAR(50), Age INT, Email VARCHAR(50), HighScore INT);</t><s>UPSERT INTO PlayerGameHistory (PlayerID, GameID, PlayTimeInHours, Score) VALUES (1, 1, 10, 500) ON DUPLICATE KEY UPDATE PlayTimeInHours = 10, Score = 500;</s>
